name:F‚Äça‚Äçy‚Äçc‚Äçh‚Äço‚Äço
info:Deluxe King Room
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Friends
info:3 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted April 15, 2024
msg:As the only three-tower building in Nanjing Jiangbei area, the Golden Eagle G Hotel is a landmark building, with an excellent location overlooking the city and convenient transportation. The overall style of the hotel is Chinese business style. As soon as you enter the lobby, you can see the graceful figure of the Qinhuai beauty on the screen on the left. The hotel lobby is on the 50th floor, and the hanging window on the back of the lobby is a very distinctive metal symmetrical structure. The metal frame arch structure of the corridor opposite the lobby is based on the design of Nanjing local architecture, which is also quite flavorful. Going to the left, there is a representative restaurant of Nanjing classic Jianghuai cuisine-Pinwei Jiangnan. The entire corridor is very open. I met a newlywed couple taking pictures. Haha, it is very romantic and photogenic. The crystal wall dome is very romantic. Looking up at the sky, but unfortunately... the weather is not good. Haha, if it is a sunny sunset, it should be a different flavor.
Back to the guest room, the basic room of 40 square meters can be regarded as a large space in any star hotel. There are toilets and showers on both sides of the room, and then a small cloakroom. The smart home appliances of the toilet in the room are very convenient. The bedding is also soft enough but not lacking in support. What is more worth mentioning is that the view on the 69th floor is wide and quiet. You can experience the hustle and bustle of the city and the power of the city's emerging development brought by technological development at any time of the day or night.
In particular, in addition to the top hardware, the hotel's humanized service makes people feel at home. The hotel management is very standardized and standardized. It can be said that it is better than Marriott and Accor in this regard. It greatly protects the safety and privacy of the guests, and also meets the needs of the guest rooms in the details. This time, I chose G Hotel because I came here to admire the semi-buffet dinner at the Skyline Restaurant on the 50th floor. I chose one of the four main dishes and one of the soups. The four of us ordered two baked Boston lobster & noodles for the main course, and one fried salmon for each. And Wellington steak, everyone share, share the taste of this high-end restaurant. The most surprising thing is the small order for two consisting of caviar and foie gras.         The food is satisfied, and the stay is surprisingly good. The corner room on the 65th floor can overlook Nanjing City 180 degrees, with a wide field of vision. The Yangtze River is not far away, and the dusk and night views are super beautiful.
